<date>1522453937378< /date><rating>5< /rating>< Review>
I love this salon. The clientele is diverse and the employees are incredibly nice and good at what they do. Kelly and Lili do amazing pedicures and gel polishes. I got a new set of acrylic nails, plus gel polish and a spa pedicure for $53 the last time I was there. I've paid as much for one service at other salons for the same quality of service. They take cash and credit, though there is a $1 fee for credit. I really enjoy the employees and clientele - last time I was there there were two very manly Hispanic dudes getting pedicures, and no one batted an eyelid. Very nice people, good product, good prices. Call ahead to see if they are busy if you don't want to wait and they will take care of you when you come over.</Review>

<rate>4< /rate><Pictures>None<//Pictures>< username>
Ed Miller<//username>
< Text>
The whole made-to-order liquid nitrogen ice cream thing seems pretty commonplace these days. Like some other places, there are lots of choices for the base ice cream as well as flavors and toppings. The exciting thing for me were the non-dairy options: sorbet and coconut. I ordered a Quantum Coffee with the coconut base.

The price is on the high side for ice cream, but not too surprising for specialty ice cream. After ordering I sat to to wait... for a while. There were very few customers, so I was surprised at how long it took. I don't remember waiting so long at similar places. The final product was really good. It was probably one of the best coconut ice creams that I've had.

I probably would have given a 5 star rating if the wait time were shorter, or at least provide some warning or a little interaction from the staff or something. Over all, a good experience.</Text>

This is a memorial to the desert riders, those who spent time riding the desert trails on dirt bikes, quads, side by sides, 4x4's and anything else they could take out into nature.  My uncle spent years riding the local desert with his friends. This last weekend we all took a ride out to Husky to spread his ashes and place his memorial. Everyone we came upon was respectful, kind and out doing the same thing my uncle loved. Ride on Uncle Bryce!</Text>

The pro football game time food specials are good and I usually order from that menu. There is one large projection screen and several televisions in the bar area which gives a good view from anywhere.

If you're looking for a quieter place to watch football on Sunday; this is the place.</review>< Pics>

<review>This was my first time eating eating at this particular Hooley's. It was lunch time and wasn't overly busy. But my server, Galin was serving at least 15 others and I am giving her and the food a 5 stars all day!

I ordered the wings with a side of fries. Even though I would have preferred my wings tossed in sauce.. there was no need to. The wings were soft with a light crisp on the outside with just the right amount of seasoning. I am so happy they didn't come wet. I asked for Buffalo, BBQ and the Suicide Habanero sauce. These sauces made the wings even more enjoyable. Can't go wrong there.

The fries went well with the taste of the wings. Nice and thick steak fries with some light seasoning.... And a really good size portion too. (I can't count how many times I go to a wing place and they serve up the craziest, soggy or burnt fries.)These were legit.

Back to Galin's service, everytime I needed a refill of my ice tea she got me, before I asked.. and when I asked for something she responded super quick. Even though she was running around she made sure I was taken care of. This place was on point.

Definitely coming back to this spot.< /review></record></dataset><record>
